     <div class="articleWide cleared">
      <div class="alpha">
       <div class="article-text wide" id="js-article-text">
        <h1>
         Taking over-the-counter allergy pills 'can cause memory problems for pensioners'
        </h1>
        <ul>
         <li style="font-weight: bold;">
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           Canadian scientists say allergy pills can hit memory of older people
          </font>
         </li>
         <li>
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Drugs for depression and insomnia also linked to concentration loss
           </span>
          </font>
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p class="author-section byline-plain">
         By
         <a class="author" href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Sophie+Borland+for+the+Daily+Mail" rel="nofollow">
          Sophie Borland for the Daily Mail
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="byline-section">
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Published:
          </span>
          19:58 EST, 11 November 2012
         </span>
         |
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Updated:
          </span>
          02:59 EST, 12 November 2012
         </span>
        </p>
        <div id="articleIconLinksContainer">
         <ul>
          <li class="share-facebook">
          </li>
          <li class="share-twitter">
          </li>
          <li class="share-pinterest">
          </li>
          <li class="share-gplus">
           <span class="g-interactivepost" data-calltoactionlabel="VIEW" data-calltoactionurl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-2231565/Taking-counter-allergy-pills-cause-memory-problems-pensioners.html" data-clientid="746589970956-e10ciaf67a1id9ggu75ph3ds0sthn7j6.apps.googleusercontent.com" data-contentdeeplinkid="/pages" data-contenturl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-2231565/Taking-counter-allergy-pills-cause-memory-problems-pensioners.html" data-cookiepolicy="single_host_origin" data-prefilltext="Taking over-the-counter allergy pills 'can cause memory problems for pensioners'">
            <a>
            </a>
           </span>
          </li>
          <li class="share-email">
           <a class="js-email" data-ajax-refresh-everytime="true" data-modal-id="email-modal-overlay" data-modal-type="email-overlay" data-on-mobile="mailto:?subject=Taking over-the-counter allergy pills 'can cause memory problems for pensioners'&amp;body=http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-2231565/Taking-counter-allergy-pills-cause-memory-problems-pensioners.html" data-placement="top" data-target="/email-article.html?id=2231565" data-toggle="modal" href="#email" title="Email to a friend">
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="share-icons" id="shareLinkTop">
           <a class="js-sl share-link" href="#socialLinks">
           </a>
           <script type="text/javascript">

         <a class="comments-count home" href="/health/article-2231565/Taking-counter-allergy-pills-cause-memory-problems-pensioners.html#comments">
          <span>
          </span>
          <p class="count-number">
           23
          </p>

           View
           <br/>

         <script>

        });
         </script>
        </div>
        <div class="floatRHS">
         <img alt="Risks: Common allergy medicines have been found to cause memory and concentration problems in older people, researchers say. Picture posed by model" class="blkBorder" height="461" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/11/12/article-0-0D1040A300000578-336_306x461.jpg" width="306"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Risks: Common allergy medicines have been found to cause memory and concentration problems in older people, researchers say. Picture posed by model
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Allergy pills taken by thousands of Britons could be causing memory problems, researchers claim.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Common treatments including Benadryl for hayfever have been found to increase forgetfulness and concentration difficulties in pensioners.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Canadian scientists have also found a link with popular sleeping pills and antidepressants.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          They are now urging doctors to consider whether their patients should really be taking these medications in light of the possible side-effects.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Although the researchers did not look at the risk of dementia, there is some evidence having mild memory problems makes you far more susceptible to the devastating illness.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Academics from Montreal University in Canada looked at 68 studies which had examined the potential health risks of certain medications.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          They found that treatments for allergies, insomnia, depression and for overactive bladders were all linked to memory and concentration problems.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          These drugs include Benadryl, for hayfever, benzodiazepines such as the sleeping pills diazepam and temazepam and the antidepressant amitriptyline.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Lead researcher Dr Cara Tannenbaum warned that the potential effects of such drugs on memory problems, or cognitive decline, is undervalued.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          She said: Patients need this information so that they are more comfortable talking to their doctors and pharmacists about safer pharmacological or non-pharmacological treatment options.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Each individual has a right to make an informed choice based on preference and a thorough understanding of the effects the medications may have on their memory and function.
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="related-carousel with-fb health half" data-track-module="am-related_carousel^related_carousel" data-track-pos="static" data-track-selector=".rotator-panels a:not([class*=external])" id="p-16">

          <h2>
           Share this article
          </h2>
          <div class="share">
           <span class="wai">
            Share
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

   });
 });
        </script>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          The study, published in the journal Drugs and Aging, concluded: Patients are increasingly concerned with perceived memory and attention deficits that may signal early dementia.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          The impact of medications on cognitive function and their ability to affect the results of neuropsychological test scores during the clinical assessment of memory complaints is undervalued.
         </font>
         <br/>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Recall: Having mild memory problems can make elderly people more susceptible to dementia" class="blkBorder" height="417" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/11/12/article-2231565-11D51D64000005DC-932_634x417.jpg" width="634"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Recall: Having mild memory problems can make elderly people more susceptible to dementia, evidence suggests
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          There is a consistent body of evidence suggesting that drug-induced mild cognitive impairment can occur with episodic use of medications for insomnia, anxiety or allergy symptoms.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Experts think the drugs interfere with chemicals in the brain called neurotransmitters, which are responsible for passing on messages.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          This may result in forgetfulness, concentration problems and there is some evidence it leads to dementia.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Earlier this year Harvard researchers found that benzodiazepines increased the risk of developing the devastating illness by up to 50 per cent.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Most antihistamine tablets are sold over the counter and there are no figures for the numbers of patients currently using them.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          But as many as 15 million Britons suffer from some form of allergy in their lives, including hayfever, although not all will seek treatment.
         </font>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Figures also show that around 1.5 million are on sleeping pills and 6 million on antidepressants.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '&lt;div id="' + id + '"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
            $(node).after(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=health&amp;pageSize=10',
            total: 13.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
       </script>

    });
});
        </script>
